<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebber</a></i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebber</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebbers.html>liefhebbers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liefhebber.html>liefhebbertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">liefhebster</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fan, enthusiast

<li>amateur, dilettante</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a lover, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:loves.html>loves</a> someone or something</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lier.html>lier</a> (26602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:lyra.html>lyra</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λύρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a> (486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ligjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*legʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie; to be lying down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often of place names</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be, to be placed or located
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rommel.html>rommel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zolder.html>zolder</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> a lot of rubbish in the attic.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> Geldrop <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Could you tell <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> where Geldrop <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> (located)</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms a continuous aspect. Although it <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> an implication of lying, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> vague and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not emphasized.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biefstuk.html>biefstuk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Your <a href = vnd.unilang:steak.html>steak</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> (lying)</b> there getting cold.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ligging.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>ligging</a> (30421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ligginge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>ligging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>liggingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>geographical position, stressing in particular the relation to the surroundings or the orientation of an object; location, lie, situation</li>
<li>the position of an unborn mammal in the womb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the act or state of lying, reclination</li></ol>

***ligstoel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ligstoel.html>ligstoel</a> (60236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligstoel.html>ligstoel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligstoelen.html>ligstoelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligstoel.html>ligstoeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A lounger, a lounging chair.</li></ol>

***lijden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijden.html>lijden</a> (1761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">līthan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līþaną</i>. The sense developed from “go, travel” <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> “endure” to “suffer”, under the influence of the originally unrelated noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leed.html>leed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See the same in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijden.html>lijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to undergo</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffer [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span>(object)</span></span> = from (a disease)]</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">suffering</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leed.html>leed</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">lijdenis</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a> (1002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*līk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līką</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">lyk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leiche</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:lig.html>lig</a></i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*līg-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkje.html>lijkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The dead but otherwise (mostly) intact body of a human or animal; corpse</li></ol>

***lijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a> (820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geliken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gilīkon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galīkōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>lijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem, appear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkt.html>lijkt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leuk.html>leuk</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b>seems</b> fun (to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>)!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look like, resemble (depict well what it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> intended to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekening.html>tekening</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkt.html>lijkt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:sprekend.html>sprekend</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This drawing <b><a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a></b> just like the real thing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">liken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">līcon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līkāną</i>.

***lijkenpikker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijkenpikker.html>lijkenpikker</a> (69009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pikker</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkenpikker.html>lijkenpikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkenpikkers.html>lijkenpikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkenpikker.html>lijkenpikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who benefits from others' misery.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a living from funerals or tending to the dead in any other way.</li></ol>

***lijkrede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijkrede.html>lijkrede</a> (81801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijk.html>lijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corpse, dead body</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rede.html>rede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">discourse, speech</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leichrede</i>. First attested in the late seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkrede.html>lijkrede</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijkrede.html>lijkredes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">lijkredenen</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">lijkredens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">eulogy</span>, discourse or sermon <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> at a funeral</li></ol>

***lijmen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijmen.html>lijmen</a> (23775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">limen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijm.html>lijm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, with many Indo-European cognates (e.g. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leem.html>leem</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slijm.html>slijm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slime</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), apparently from a root meaning “to smear”.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijmen.html>lijmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To glue, join (as) with glue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To convince, win <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijmde.html>lijmde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bengels.html>bengels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snoep.html>snoep</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:rascals.html>rascals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> with candy</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Unknown, perhaps the above in the sense “to string notes”.

***lijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a> (1058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">līne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*līna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līnǭ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*līno-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flax</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijnen.html>lijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijntje.html>lijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A line.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:streep.html>streep</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any line or curve.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijnen.html>lijnen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lelijk.html>lelijk</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>lines</b> in the painting <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> very ugly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A rope, a cable.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:touw.html>touw</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draad.html>draad</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabel.html>kabel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A route, a line (of transport, especially of public transport and airlines).
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">route</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A leash for restraining animals.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>Honden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> park <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dogs must be kept on a <b>leash</b> in the park.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiband.html>leiband</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A file.</li>
<li>A diet.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My children are on a <b>diet</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Short for <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waslijn.html>waslijn</a></i></span></span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangt.html>hangt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broeken.html>broeken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hanging the trousers on the <b>clothesline</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Short for <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:telefoonlijn.html>telefoonlijn</a></i></span></span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>Hallo</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on the <b>line</b>? Hello? Hello?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually  diminutive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A line of <a href = vnd.unilang:drugs.html>drugs</a> in powder form.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lijstre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">songbird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*lī(h)strō</i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laikaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move about</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***lim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>lim</a> (39270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_5">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*limą</i>, probably related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liþu-</i> (whence <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">liþ</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">limr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>lim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">limu</b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Old_English-limb"> limb, bodily member; branch (of tree etc)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_5">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*līmaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lei-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">līm</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijm.html>lijm</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">līm</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Leim</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">lím</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>lim</a></i>). The Proto-Indo-European root <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līmus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">līm</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">līmas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Old_English-glue"> glue; mortar, paste, lime</li></ol>
